                $(function(){
                        var oContent = $(".LayoutWrap>.ContentWrap>.Content"),
                                adLeft = $(".LifeOwnerGlobalLeft"),
                                adRight = $(".LifeOwnerGlobalRight");

                        var resizeTimeout = null;
                        var rs = function(){
                                var oSummonerContent = $("#SummonerLayoutContent"),
                                        oPageHeaderWrap = $(".PageHeaderWrap"),
                                        oChampionStatsMenu = $('.l-champion-statistics-menu'),
                                        oChampionIndexContent = $('.l-champion-index-content'),
                                        adTopFix = 60,
                                        adSideFix = 0;

                                if (oSummonerContent.length > 0) {
                                        var offset = oSummonerContent.offset();
                                        adTopFix += offset.top - 100;
                                        adSideFix = -675;
                                } else if (oPageHeaderWrap.length > 0) {
                                        var offset = oPageHeaderWrap.offset();
                                        adTopFix += offset.top - 100;
                                        adSideFix = -675;
                                } else if (oChampionStatsMenu.length > 0) {
                                        var offset = oChampionStatsMenu.offset();
                                        adTopFix += offset.top + 10;
                                        adSideFix = -675;
                                }else if (oChampionIndexContent.length > 0) {
                                        var offset = oChampionIndexContent.offset();
                                        adTopFix = offset.top;
                                        adSideFix = -675;
                                }

                                if (adSideFix) {
                                        adLeft.css({
                                                display: 'block',
                                                top: adTopFix
                                        });
                                        adRight.css({
                                                display: 'block',
                                                top: adTopFix
                                        });
                                } else {
                                        adLeft.css({
                                                display: 'block',
                                                top: adTopFix
                                        });
                                        adRight.css({
                                                display: 'block',
                                                top: adTopFix
                                        });
                                }

                        };

                        $(window).bind('resize', function(){
                                adLeft[0].style.display = 'none';

                                }

                                }
                        });

                });

    placementContainer.innerHTML = '<iframe id="vmv2-frm-'+id+'" src="javascript:\'<html><body></body></html>\'" width="1" height="1" data-id="'+id+'" data-site-id="59776d4146e0fb00010596c3" data-placement-id="59776e0d46e0fb00010596c7">';
    var loaderFrame = document.getElementById("vmv2-frm-"+id);
    var loaderFrameWindow = loaderFrame.contentWindow ? loaderFrame.contentWindow  : loaderFrame.contentDocument;
    loaderFrameWindow.document.open();
    loaderFrameWindow.document.write('<scr'+'ipt src="//hb.vntsm.com/v2/live/hb.js" type="text/javascript" async>'+'</scr'+'ipt>');
    loaderFrameWindow.document.close();
  };
  window['build-'+id]();
})();
</script>

                        <style>
        .SelectMatchTypes,
        .ChampionMatchSearchWrap > .Content { display: none; }

<script>

        $(function(){
                var wrap = $('.ChampionMatchSearchWrap'),
                                content = $('>.Content', wrap),
                                allChampionList = $(">.SelectMatchChampionList >.Item.All .ChampionList", content);

                var searchInputPast = null;
                var doubleChosungArray = {
                        'ã³': 'ã±ã',
                        'ãµ': 'ã´ã',
                        'ã¶': 'ã´ã',
                        'ãº': 'ã¹ã±',
                        'ã»': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã¼': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã½': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã¾': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã¿': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã': 'ã¹ã',
                        'ã': 'ãã'
                };

                var updateSearchKeyword = function(oSearchInput){
                        var keyword = oSearchInput.val().toLowerCase();
                        var allChampionHeader = $(">.AllChampion", allChampionList);
                        var allChampions = $(">.Item", allChampionList);

                        if (keyword.length > 0) {
                                allChampionHeader.show();
                        }

//                              if (keyword == searchInputPast) {
//                                      return;
//                              }

                        for (var doubleChosung in doubleChosungArray) {
                                if (doubleChosungArray.hasOwnProperty(doubleChosung)) {
                                        var spritedChosung = doubleChosungArray[doubleChosung];
                                        keyword = keyword.replaceAll(doubleChosung, spritedChosung);
                                }
                        }

                        searchInputPast = keyword;

                        allChampions.each(function(i, o){
                                var championName = $(o).data('champion-name'),
                                                championKey = $(o).data('champion-key'),
                                                championNameChosung = $(o).data('champion-name-chosung');

                                if (championName) {
                                        if (championName.indexOf(keyword) >= 0 || championKey.indexOf(keyword) >= 0 || (championNameChosung && championNameChosung.indexOf(keyword) >= 0)) {
                                                $(o).removeClass('hide');
                                                $(o).addClass('show');
                                        } else {
                                                $(o).removeClass('show');
                                                $(o).addClass('hide');
                                        }
                                }
                        });

                        var championNotFound = $(">.ChampionNotFound", allChampionList);
                        if ($(">.Item.show", allChampionList).length == 0) {
                                championNotFound.show();
                        } else {
                                championNotFound.hide();
                        }
                };

                var showChampionMatchSearch = function(){
                                        // ì¤ë³µ ì´ë²¤í¸ í ë¹ ë¬¸ì 
                                        if (content.is(':visible')) {
                                                return;
                                        }

                                        content.show();
                                        $(document).on('click', function(event){
                                                var target = event.target || event.srcElement;
                                                if (!$(target).closest(wrap.selector).length) {
                                                        hideChampionMatchSearch();
                                                }
                                        });
                                },
                                hideChampionMatchSearch = function(){
                                        content.hide();
                                        $(document).off('click');
                                };

                // ìë¬´í¤ë ëë¥´ë©´ ëìì£¼ëë¡
                var searchInput = $('>.Header >.Input', wrap);
                searchInput
                                .on('keyup keydown change click', function(){
                                        showChampionMatchSearch();
                                        updateSearchKeyword($(this));
                                        ga('send', 'event', 'button', 'OpenChampionSearchInMatch');
                                });
        });
</script>

                                        $(function() {
                                                $('.SelectMatchChampionList').on('click', ' .ChampionList .Item>a', function(evt) {
                                                        evt.preventDefault();
                                                        var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                                                        $.OP.GG.matches.list.changeChampion($this.data('champion-id'), $this);
                                                });

        <script>
                $(function() {
                        var $gameItemList = $('.GameListContainer');

                        $gameItemList.on('click', '.AlertMessageButton .Button', function(evt) {
                                evt.preventDefault();
                                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                                if ($this.hasClass('Blue')) {
                                        $.OP.GG.summoner.renewBtn.start(evt.currentTarget, summonerId);
                                } else if ($this.hasClass('Green')) {
                                        $.OP.GG.summoner.RequireRenewMatch(summonerId, gameId, evt.currentTarget);
                                }
                        });

                        $gameItemList.on('click', '.OpenBuildButton', function(evt) {
                                evt.preventDefault();
                                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                                $.OP.GG.matches.openBuild(gameId, summonerId, $gameItem);
                        });

                        $gameItemList.on('click', '.OpenSpectateButton', function(evt) {
                                evt.preventDefault();
                                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');

                                $.OP.GG.matches.openSpectate(gameId);
                        });

                        $gameItemList.on('click', '.Button.MatchDetail', function(evt) {
                                evt.preventDefault();
                                var $this = $(evt.currentTarget);
                                var $gameItem = $this.closest('.GameItem');
                                var summonerId = $gameItem.data('summoner-id');
                                var gameId = $gameItem.data('game-id');
                                var gameTime = $gameItem.data('game-time');

                                $.OP.GG.matches.openDetail(gameId, summonerId, $gameItem, gameTime);
                        })
                });
        </script>

                (function() {
                        var id = "59776e0246e0fb00010596c5-" + Math.random().toString().replace('0.','');
                        document.write('<div id="vmv2-'+id+'"></div>');
                        window['build-'+id] = function(){
                                var placementContainer = document.getElementById("vmv2-"+id);
                                placementContainer.innerHTML = '<iframe id="vmv2-frm-'+id+'" src="javascript:\'<html><body></body></html>\'" width="1" height="1" data-id="'+id+'" data-site-id="59776d4146e0fb00010596c3" data-placement-id="59776e0246e0fb00010596c5"></iframe>';
                                var loaderFrame = document.getElementById("vmv2-frm-"+id);
                                var loaderFrameWindow = loaderFrame.contentWindow ? loaderFrame.contentWindow  : loaderFrame.contentDocument;
                                loaderFrameWindow.document.open();
                                loaderFrameWindow.document.write('<scr'+'ipt src="//hb.vntsm.com/v2/live/hb.js" type="text/javascript" async>'+'</scr'+'ipt>');
                                loaderFrameWindow.document.close();
                        };
                        window['build-'+id]();
                })();
        </script>
